```cpp
using TimePoint = Clock::time_point;

// ===== Constants =====
enum PieceType : int { NO_PIECE_TYPE = 0, PAWN = 1, KNIGHT = 2, BISHOP = 3, ROOK = 4, QUEEN = 5, KING = 6 };
enum Color : int { WHITE = 0, BLACK = 1 };
enum Piece : int { EMPTY = 0, W_PAWN = 1, W_KNIGHT = 2, W_BISHOP = 3, W_ROOK = 4, W_QUEEN = 5, W_KING = 6,
                   B_PAWN = 7, B_KNIGHT = 8, B_BISHOP = 9, B_ROOK = 10, B_QUEEN = 11, B_KING = 12 };
enum TTFlag : uint8_t { TT_EXACT = 0, TT_LOWER = 1, TT_UPPER = 2 };
enum MoveFlag : int { FLAG_NONE = 0, FLAG_EP = 1, FLAG_CASTLE = 2, FLAG_DOUBLE = 4 };

inline int makePiece(int color, int type) { return color * 6 + type; }
inline int pieceType(int p) { return p == 0 ? 0 : ((p - 1) % 6) + 1; }
inline int pieceColor(int p) { return p == 0 ? 0 : (p - 1) / 6; }
inline bool isWhite(int p) { return p >= 1 && p <= 6; }
inline bool isBlack(int p) { return p >= 7 && p <= 12; }
inline int makeSquare(int rank, int file) { return (rank << 3) | file; }
inline int rankOf(int sq) { return sq >> 3; }
inline int fileOf(int sq) { return sq & 7; }

string squareStr(int sq) {
    return string(1, 'a' + fileOf(sq)) + string(1, '1' + rankOf(sq));
}

char pieceChar(int pt) {
    static const char chars[] = { '?', 'p', 'N', 'B', 'R', 'Q', 'K' };
    return chars[pt];
}

char promotionChar(int pt) {
    static const char chars[] = { '?', '?', 'N', 'B', 'R', 'Q', '?' };
    return chars[pt];
}

// Material values
const int MATERIAL[] = { 0, 100, 320, 330, 500, 900, 20000 };

// ===== Move =====
struct Move {
    int from, to;
    int captured;
    int promotion; // piece type (KNIGHT, BISHOP, ROOK, QUEEN) or 0
    int flags;
    
    bool isEnPassant() const { return flags & FLAG_EP; }
    bool isCastling() const { return flags & FLAG_CASTLE; }
    bool isDoublePush() const { return flags & FLAG_DOUBLE; }
    bool isCapture() const { return captured != 0 || isEnPassant(); }
    bool isPromotion() const { return promotion != 0; }
    
    bool operator==(const Move& o) const {
        return from == o.from && to == o.to && promotion == o.promotion && flags == o.flags;
    }
};

// Compact move for TT
typedef uint32_t CompactMove;
CompactMove packMove(const Move& m) {
    return (uint32_t)m.from | ((uint32_t)m.to << 6) | ((uint32_t)m.promotion << 12) | 
           ((uint32_t)(m.flags & 3) << 15);
}
Move unpackMove(CompactMove cm) {
    Move m;
    m.from = cm & 63;
    m.to = (cm >> 6) & 63;
    m.promotion = (cm >> 12) & 7;
    m.flags = (cm >> 15) & 3;
    m.captured = 0;
    return m;
}

// ===== Zobrist Keys =====
uint64_t zobPiece[13][64];
uint64_t zobCastling[16];
uint64_t zobEp[8];
uint64_t zobSide;

void initZobrist() {
    // Use a simple PRNG for reproducibility
    uint64_t seed = 0x1234567890ABCDEFULL;
    auto rng = [&]() {
        seed ^= seed << 13;
        seed ^= seed >> 7;
        seed ^= seed << 17;
        return seed;
    };
    
    for (int p = 1; p <= 12; p++)
        for (int sq = 0; sq < 64; sq++)
            zobPiece[p][sq] = rng();
    
    for (int i = 0; i < 16; i++)
        zobCastling[i] = rng();
    
    for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
        zobEp[i] = rng();
    
    zobSide = rng();
}

// ===== Piece-Square Tables =====
// From White's perspective (rank 0 = 1st rank)
const int PST_PAWN[64] = {
      0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,
     50, 50, 50, 50, 50, 50, 50, 50,
     10, 10, 20, 30, 30, 20, 10, 10,
      5,  5, 10, 25, 25, 10,  5,  5,
      0,  0,  0, 20, 20,  0,  0,  0,
      5, -5,-10,  0,  0,-10, -5,  5,
      5, 10, 10,-20,-20, 10, 10,  5,
      0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0
};

const int PST_KNIGHT[64] = {
    -50,-40,-30,-30,-30,-30,-40,-50,
    -40,-20,  0,  0,  0,  0,-20,-40,
    -30,  0, 10, 15, 15, 10,  0,-30,
    -30,  5, 15, 20, 20, 15,  5,-30,
    -30,  0, 15, 20, 20, 15,  0,-30,
    -30,  5, 10, 15, 15, 10,  5,-30,
    -40,-20,  0,  5,  5,  0,-20,-40,
    -50,-40,-30,-30,-30,-30,-40,-50
};

const int PST_BISHOP[64] = {
    -20,-10,-10,-10,-10,-10,-10,-20,
    -10,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,-10,
    -10,  0, 10, 10, 10, 10,  0,-10,
    -10,  5,  5, 10, 10,  5,  5,-10,
    -10,  0, 10, 10, 10, 10,  0,-10,
    -10, 10, 10, 10, 10, 10, 10,-10,
    -10,  5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  5,-10,
    -20,-10,-10,-10,-10,-10,-10,-20
};

const int PST_ROOK[64] = {
      0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,
      5, 10, 10, 10, 10, 10, 10,  5,
     -5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0, -5,
     -5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0, -5,
     -5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0, -5,
     -5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0, -5,
     -5,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0, -5,
      0,  0,  0,  5,  5,  0,  0,  0
};

const int PST_QUEEN[64] = {
    -20,-10,-10, -5, -5,-10,-10,-20,
    -10,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,  0,-10,
    -10,  0,  5,  5,  5,  5,  0,-10,
     -5,  0,  5,  5,  5,  5,  0, -5,
      0,  0,  5,  5,  5,  5,  0, -5,
    -10,  5,  5,  5,  5,  5,  0,-10,
    -10,  0,  5,  0,  0,  0,  0,-10,
    -20,-10,-10, -5, -5,-10,-10,-20
};

const int PST_KING_MG[64] = {
    -30,-40,-40,-50,-50,-40,-40,-30,
    -30,-40,-40,-50,-50,-40,-40,-30,
    -30,-40,-40,-50,-50,-40,-40,-30,
    -30,-40,-40,-50,-50,-40,-40,-30,
    -20,-30,-30,-40,-40,-30,-30,-20,
    -10,-20,-20,-20,-20,-20,-20,-10,
     20, 20,  0,  0,  0,  0, 20, 20,
     20, 30, 10,  0,  0, 10, 30, 20
};

const int* PST[] = { nullptr, PST_PAWN, PST_KNIGHT, PST_BISHOP, PST_ROOK, PST_QUEEN, PST_KING_MG };

// Mirror square for black's perspective
inline int mirrorSquare(int sq) { return sq ^ 56; }

// ===== Position =====
struct UndoInfo {
    int captured;
    int castling;
    int epSquare;
    int halfmove;
    uint64_t hash;
};

class Position {
public:
    int board[64];
    int side; // side to move
    int castling; // castling rights (4 bits)
    int epSquare; // en passant target square (-1 if none)
    int halfmove;
    int fullmove;
    uint64_t hash;
    int kingSq[2];
    
    UndoInfo undoStack[1024];
    int undoCount;
    
    Position() : side(WHITE), castling(0), epSquare(-1), halfmove(0), fullmove(1), hash(0), undoCount(0) {
        memset(board, 0, sizeof(board));
        kingSq[0] = kingSq[1] = -1;
    }
    
    void parseFEN(const string& fen) {
        memset(board, 0, sizeof(board));
        kingSq[0] = kingSq[1] = -1;
        undoCount = 0;
        castling = 0;
        epSquare = -1;
        
        int rank = 7, file = 0;
        size_t i = 0;
        
        // Piece placement
        while (i < fen.size() && fen[i] != ' ') {
            if (fen[i] == '/') {
                rank--;
                file = 0;
            } else if (fen[i] >= '1' && fen[i] <= '8') {
                file += fen[i] - '0';
            } else {
                int piece = charToPiece(fen[i]);
                int sq = makeSquare(rank, file);
                board[sq] = piece;
                if (pieceType(piece) == KING)
                    kingSq[pieceColor(piece)] = sq;
                file++;
            }
            i++;
        }
        i++; // skip space
        
        // Active color
        side = (fen[i] == 'w') ? WHITE : BLACK;
        i += 2; // skip color and space
        
        // Castling availability
        while (i < fen.size() && fen[i] != ' ') {
            switch (fen[i]) {
                case 'K': castling |= 1; break;
                case 'Q': castling |= 2; break;
                case 'k': castling |= 4; break;
                case 'q': castling |= 8; break;
            }
            i++;
        }
        i++; // skip space
        
        // En passant target square
        if (i < fen.size() && fen[i] == '-') {
            epSquare = -1;
            i++;
        } else if (i < fen.size()) {
            int epFile = fen[i] - 'a';
            int epRank = fen[i+1] - '1';
            epSquare = makeSquare(epRank, epFile);
            i += 2;
        }
        
        // Skip space
        if (i < fen.size() && fen[i] == ' ') i++;
        
        // Halfmove clock
        halfmove = 0;
        while (i < fen.size() && fen[i] != ' ') {
            halfmove = halfmove * 10 + (fen[i] - '0');
            i++;
        }
        
        // Skip space
        if (i < fen.size() && fen[i] == ' ') i++;
        
        // Fullmove number
        fullmove = 0;
        while (i < fen.size() && fen[i] >= '0' && fen[i] <= '9') {
            fullmove = fullmove * 10 + (fen[i] - '0');
            i++;
        }
        
        computeHash();
    }
    
    int charToPiece(char c) const {
        switch (c) {
            case 'P': return W_PAWN;
            case 'N': return W_KNIGHT;
            case 'B': return W_BISHOP;
            case 'R': return W_ROOK;
            case 'Q': return W_QUEEN;
            case 'K': return W_KING;
            case 'p': return B_PAWN;
            case 'n': return B_KNIGHT;
            case 'b': return B_BISHOP;
            case 'r': return B_ROOK;
            case 'q': return B_QUEEN;
            case 'k': return B_KING;
            default: return EMPTY;
        }
    }
    
    void computeHash() {
        hash = 0;
        for (int sq = 0; sq < 64; sq++) {
            if (board[sq] != EMPTY)
                hash ^= zobPiece[board[sq]][sq];
        }
        hash ^= zobCastling[castling];
        if (epSquare >= 0) hash ^= zobEp[fileOf(epSquare)];
        if (side == BLACK) hash ^= zobSide;
    }
    
    // ===== Attack Detection =====
    bool isSquareAttacked(int sq, int byColor) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        
        // Pawn attacks
        if (byColor == WHITE) {
            if (r > 0 && f > 0 && board[sq - 9] == W_PAWN) return true;
            if (r > 0 && f < 7 && board[sq - 7] == W_PAWN) return true;
        } else {
            if (r < 7 && f > 0 && board[sq + 7] == B_PAWN) return true;
            if (r < 7 && f < 7 && board[sq + 9] == B_PAWN) return true;
        }
        
        // Knight attacks
        int knight = makePiece(byColor, KNIGHT);
        static const int knightDr[] = {-2, -2, -1, -1, 1, 1, 2, 2};
        static const int knightDf[] = {-1, 1, -2, 2, -2, 2, -1, 1};
        for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
            int nr = r + knightDr[i], nf = f + knightDf[i];
            if (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8 && board[makeSquare(nr, nf)] == knight)
                return true;
        }
        
        // King attacks
        int king = makePiece(byColor, KING);
        for (int dr = -1; dr <= 1; dr++)
            for (int df = -1; df <= 1; df++) {
                if (dr == 0 && df == 0) continue;
                int nr = r + dr, nf = f + df;
                if (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8 && board[makeSquare(nr, nf)] == king)
                    return true;
            }
        
        // Bishop/Queen attacks (diagonals)
        int bishop = makePiece(byColor, BISHOP);
        int queen = makePiece(byColor, QUEEN);
        static const int diagDr[] = {-1, -1, 1, 1};
        static const int diagDf[] = {-1, 1, -1, 1};
        for (int d = 0; d < 4; d++) {
            int nr = r + diagDr[d], nf = f + diagDf[d];
            while (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8) {
                int p = board[makeSquare(nr, nf)];
                if (p != EMPTY) {
                    if (p == bishop || p == queen) return true;
                    break;
                }
                nr += diagDr[d];
                nf += diagDf[d];
            }
        }
        
        // Rook/Queen attacks (straights)
        int rook = makePiece(byColor, ROOK);
        static const int straightDr[] = {-1, 1, 0, 0};
        static const int straightDf[] = {0, 0, -1, 1};
        for (int d = 0; d < 4; d++) {
            int nr = r + straightDr[d], nf = f + straightDf[d];
            while (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8) {
                int p = board[makeSquare(nr, nf)];
                if (p != EMPTY) {
                    if (p == rook || p == queen) return true;
                    break;
                }
                nr += straightDr[d];
                nf += straightDf[d];
            }
        }
        
        return false;
    }
    
    bool inCheck() const {
        return isSquareAttacked(kingSq[side], side ^ 1);
    }
    
    // ===== Move Generation =====
    void addMove(vector<Move>& moves, int from, int to, int captured, int promotion, int flags) const {
        moves.push_back({from, to, captured, promotion, flags});
    }
    
    void generatePawnMoves(vector<Move>& moves, int sq) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        int dir = (side == WHITE) ? 1 : -1;
        int startRank = (side == WHITE) ? 1 : 6;
        int promoRank = (side == WHITE) ? 7 : 0;
        int piece = makePiece(side, PAWN);
        
        // Single push
        int nr = r + dir;
        if (nr >= 0 && nr < 8) {
            int to = makeSquare(nr, f);
            if (board[to] == EMPTY) {
                if (nr == promoRank) {
                    // Promotion
                    for (int pt = KNIGHT; pt <= QUEEN; pt++)
                        addMove(moves, sq, to, EMPTY, pt, FLAG_NONE);
                } else {
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                    
                    // Double push
                    if (r == startRank) {
                        int to2 = makeSquare(r + 2 * dir, f);
                        if (board[to2] == EMPTY)
                            addMove(moves, sq, to2, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_DOUBLE);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Captures
        for (int df = -1; df <= 1; df += 2) {
            int nf = f + df;
            if (nf < 0 || nf >= 8) continue;
            int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
            if (nr < 0 || nr >= 8) continue;
            
            int target = board[to];
            if (target != EMPTY && pieceColor(target) != side) {
                if (nr == promoRank) {
                    for (int pt = KNIGHT; pt <= QUEEN; pt++)
                        addMove(moves, sq, to, target, pt, FLAG_NONE);
                } else {
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                }
            }
            
            // En passant
            if (to == epSquare) {
                int capturedSq = makeSquare(r, nf);
                int capturedPiece = board[capturedSq];
                addMove(moves, sq, to, capturedPiece, 0, FLAG_EP);
            }
        }
    }
    
    void generateKnightMoves(vector<Move>& moves, int sq) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        static const int dr[] = {-2, -2, -1, -1, 1, 1, 2, 2};
        static const int df[] = {-1, 1, -2, 2, -2, 2, -1, 1};
        int piece = makePiece(side, KNIGHT);
        
        for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
            int nr = r + dr[i], nf = f + df[i];
            if (nr < 0 || nr >= 8 || nf < 0 || nf >= 8) continue;
            int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
            int target = board[to];
            if (target == EMPTY || pieceColor(target) != side)
                addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
        }
    }
    
    void generateSlidingMoves(vector<Move>& moves, int sq, const int* dr, const int* df, int numDirs) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        
        for (int d = 0; d < numDirs; d++) {
            int nr = r + dr[d], nf = f + df[d];
            while (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8) {
                int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
                int target = board[to];
                if (target == EMPTY) {
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                } else {
                    if (pieceColor(target) != side)
                        addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                    break;
                }
                nr += dr[d];
                nf += df[d];
            }
        }
    }
    
    void generateKingMoves(vector<Move>& moves, int sq) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        
        for (int dr = -1; dr <= 1; dr++)
            for (int df = -1; df <= 1; df++) {
                if (dr == 0 && df == 0) continue;
                int nr = r + dr, nf = f + df;
                if (nr < 0 || nr >= 8 || nf < 0 || nf >= 8) continue;
                int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
                int target = board[to];
                if (target == EMPTY || pieceColor(target) != side)
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
            }
        
        // Castling
        if (side == WHITE) {
            if ((castling & 1) && sq == 4) { // White kingside
                if (board[5] == EMPTY && board[6] == EMPTY &&
                    board[7] == W_ROOK &&
                    !isSquareAttacked(4, BLACK) && !isSquareAttacked(5, BLACK) && !isSquareAttacked(6, BLACK))
                    addMove(moves, 4, 6, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_CASTLE);
            }
            if ((castling & 2) && sq == 4) { // White queenside
                if (board[3] == EMPTY && board[2] == EMPTY && board[1] == EMPTY &&
                    board[0] == W_ROOK &&
                    !isSquareAttacked(4, BLACK) && !isSquareAttacked(3, BLACK) && !isSquareAttacked(2, BLACK))
                    addMove(moves, 4, 2, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_CASTLE);
            }
        } else {
            if ((castling & 4) && sq == 60) { // Black kingside
                if (board[61] == EMPTY && board[62] == EMPTY &&
                    board[63] == B_ROOK &&
                    !isSquareAttacked(60, WHITE) && !isSquareAttacked(61, WHITE) && !isSquareAttacked(62, WHITE))
                    addMove(moves, 60, 62, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_CASTLE);
            }
            if ((castling & 8) && sq == 60) { // Black queenside
                if (board[59] == EMPTY && board[58] == EMPTY && board[57] == EMPTY &&
                    board[56] == B_ROOK &&
                    !isSquareAttacked(60, WHITE) && !isSquareAttacked(59, WHITE) && !isSquareAttacked(58, WHITE))
                    addMove(moves, 60, 58, EMPTY, 0, FLAG_CASTLE);
            }
        }
    }
    
    vector<Move> generatePseudoLegalMoves() const {
        vector<Move> moves;
        moves.reserve(256);
        
        for (int sq = 0; sq < 64; sq++) {
            int p = board[sq];
            if (p == EMPTY || pieceColor(p) != side) continue;
            
            int pt = pieceType(p);
            switch (pt) {
                case PAWN: generatePawnMoves(moves, sq); break;
                case KNIGHT: generateKnightMoves(moves, sq); break;
                case BISHOP: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, -1, 1, 1};
                    static const int df[] = {-1, 1, -1, 1};
                    generateSlidingMoves(moves, sq, dr, df, 4);
                    break;
                }
                case ROOK: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, 1, 0, 0};
                    static const int df[] = {0, 0, -1, 1};
                    generateSlidingMoves(moves, sq, dr, df, 4);
                    break;
                }
                case QUEEN: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, -1, -1, 0, 0, 1, 1, 1};
                    static const int df[] = {-1, 0, 1, -1, 1, -1, 0, 1};
                    generateSlidingMoves(moves, sq, dr, df, 8);
                    break;
                }
                case KING: generateKingMoves(moves, sq); break;
            }
        }
        
        return moves;
    }
    
    vector<Move> generateLegalMoves() {
        vector<Move> pseudo = generatePseudoLegalMoves();
        vector<Move> legal;
        legal.reserve(pseudo.size());
        
        for (const Move& m : pseudo) {
            makeMove(m);
            if (!isSquareAttacked(kingSq[side], side ^ 1))
                legal.push_back(m);
            unmakeMove(m);
        }
        
        return legal;
    }
    
    // Generate capture moves only (for quiescence search)
    vector<Move> generateCaptureMoves() const {
        vector<Move> moves;
        moves.reserve(64);
        
        for (int sq = 0; sq < 64; sq++) {
            int p = board[sq];
            if (p == EMPTY || pieceColor(p) != side) continue;
            
            int pt = pieceType(p);
            switch (pt) {
                case PAWN: generatePawnCaptures(moves, sq); break;
                case KNIGHT: generateKnightCaptures(moves, sq); break;
                case BISHOP: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, -1, 1, 1};
                    static const int df[] = {-1, 1, -1, 1};
                    generateSlidingCaptures(moves, sq, dr, df, 4);
                    break;
                }
                case ROOK: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, 1, 0, 0};
                    static const int df[] = {0, 0, -1, 1};
                    generateSlidingCaptures(moves, sq, dr, df, 4);
                    break;
                }
                case QUEEN: {
                    static const int dr[] = {-1, -1, -1, 0, 0, 1, 1, 1};
                    static const int df[] = {-1, 0, 1, -1, 1, -1, 0, 1};
                    generateSlidingCaptures(moves, sq, dr, df, 8);
                    break;
                }
                case KING: break; // king captures are rare and not critical for qsearch
            }
        }
        
        return moves;
    }
    
    void generatePawnCaptures(vector<Move>& moves, int sq) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        int dir = (side == WHITE) ? 1 : -1;
        int promoRank = (side == WHITE) ? 7 : 0;
        int nr = r + dir;
        if (nr < 0 || nr >= 8) return;
        
        // Forward capture directions
        for (int df = -1; df <= 1; df += 2) {
            int nf = f + df;
            if (nf < 0 || nf >= 8) continue;
            int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
            int target = board[to];
            if (target != EMPTY && pieceColor(target) != side) {
                if (nr == promoRank) {
                    for (int pt = KNIGHT; pt <= QUEEN; pt++)
                        addMove(moves, sq, to, target, pt, FLAG_NONE);
                } else {
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                }
            }
            if (to == epSquare) {
                int capturedSq = makeSquare(r, nf);
                addMove(moves, sq, to, board[capturedSq], 0, FLAG_EP);
            }
        }
        
        // Also add pawn promotions (non-capture)
        {
            int to = makeSquare(nr, f);
            if (board[to] == EMPTY && nr == promoRank) {
                for (int pt = KNIGHT; pt <= QUEEN; pt++)
                    addMove(moves, sq, to, EMPTY, pt, FLAG_NONE);
            }
        }
    }
    
    void generateKnightCaptures(vector<Move>& moves, int sq) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        static const int dr[] = {-2, -2, -1, -1, 1, 1, 2, 2};
        static const int df[] = {-1, 1, -2, 2, -2, 2, -1, 1};
        
        for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
            int nr = r + dr[i], nf = f + df[i];
            if (nr < 0 || nr >= 8 || nf < 0 || nf >= 8) continue;
            int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
            int target = board[to];
            if (target != EMPTY && pieceColor(target) != side)
                addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
        }
    }
    
    void generateSlidingCaptures(vector<Move>& moves, int sq, const int* dr, const int* df, int numDirs) const {
        int r = rankOf(sq), f = fileOf(sq);
        
        for (int d = 0; d < numDirs; d++) {
            int nr = r + dr[d], nf = f + df[d];
            while (nr >= 0 && nr < 8 && nf >= 0 && nf < 8) {
                int to = makeSquare(nr, nf);
                int target = board[to];
                if (target != EMPTY) {
                    if (pieceColor(target) != side)
                        addMove(moves, sq, to, target, 0, FLAG_NONE);
                    break;
                }
                nr += dr[d];
                nf += df[d];
            }
        }
    }
    
    // ===== Make/Unmake Move =====
    void makeMove(const Move& m) {
        UndoInfo& undo = undoStack[undoCount++];
        undo.captured = m.captured;
        undo.castling = castling;
        undo.epSquare = epSquare;
        undo.halfmove = halfmove;
        undo.hash = hash;
        
        int from = m.from, to = m.to;
        int piece = board[from];
        int pt = pieceType(piece);
        int color = pieceColor(piece);
        
        // Remove piece from source
        hash ^= zobPiece[piece][from];
        board[from] = EMPTY;
        
        // Remove captured piece
        if (m.captured != EMPTY) {
            if (m.isEnPassant()) {
                int capSq = makeSquare(rankOf(from), fileOf(to));
                hash ^= zobPiece[m.captured][capSq];
                board[capSq] = EMPTY;
            } else {
                hash ^= zobPiece[m.captured][to];
            }
        }
        
        // Place piece on destination
        if (m.isPromotion()) {
            int promoPiece = makePiece(color, m.promotion);
            hash ^= zobPiece[promoPiece][to];
            board[to] = promoPiece;
        } else {
            hash ^= zobPiece[piece][to];
            board[to] = piece;
        }
        
        // Handle castling rook
        if (m.isCastling()) {
            int rookFrom, rookTo;
            if (to > from) { // Kingside
                rookFrom = from + 3;
                rookTo = from + 1;
            } else { // Queenside
                rookFrom = from - 4;
                rookTo = from - 1;
            }
            int rook = board[rookFrom];
            hash ^= zobPiece[rook][rookFrom];
            board[rookFrom] = EMPTY;
            hash ^= zobPiece[rook][rookTo];
            board[rookTo] = rook;
        }
        
        // Update king position
        if (pt == KING)
            kingSq[color] = to;
        
        // Update castling rights
        hash ^= zobCastling[castling];
        if (pt == KING) {
            if (color == WHITE) castling &= ~3;
            else castling &= ~12;
        }
        // Rook moves or captured
        if (from == 0 || to == 0) castling &= ~2;   // a1
        if (from == 7 || to == 7) castling &= ~1;   // h1
        if (from == 56 || to == 56) castling &= ~8;  // a8
        if (from == 63 || to == 63) castling &= ~4;  // h8
        hash ^= zobCastling[castling];
        
        // Update en passant square
        hash ^= (epSquare >= 0) ? zobEp[fileOf(epSquare)] : 0;
        if (pt == PAWN && abs(rankOf(to) - rankOf(from)) == 2) {
            epSquare = makeSquare((rankOf(from) + rankOf(to)) / 2, fileOf(from));
            hash ^= zobEp[fileOf(epSquare)];
        } else {
            epSquare = -1;
        }
        
        // Update halfmove clock
        if (pt == PAWN || m.isCapture())
            halfmove = 0;
        else
            halfmove++;
        
        // Update fullmove number
        if (side == BLACK) fullmove++;
        
        // Toggle side
        hash ^= zobSide;
        side ^= 1;
    }
    
    void unmakeMove(const Move& m) {
        side ^= 1;
        const UndoInfo& undo = undoStack[--undoCount];
        
        int from = m.from, to = m.to;
        int piece = board[to];
        
        // Handle promotion: restore pawn
        if (m.isPromotion()) {
            piece = makePiece(side, PAWN);
        }
        
        // Move piece back
        board[from] = piece;
        board[to] = EMPTY;
        
        // Restore captured piece
        if (m.isEnPassant()) {
            int capSq = makeSquare(rankOf(from), fileOf(to));
            board[capSq] = m.captured;
            board[to] = EMPTY; // ep target square was empty
        } else if (m.captured != EMPTY) {
            board[to] = m.captured;
        }
        
        // Handle castling rook
        if (m.isCastling()) {
            int rookFrom, rookTo;
            if (to > from) { // Kingside
                rookFrom = from + 3;
                rookTo = from + 1;
            } else { // Queenside
                rookFrom = from - 4;
                rookTo = from - 1;
            }
            board[rookFrom] = board[rookTo];
            board[rookTo] = EMPTY;
        }
        
        // Restore king position
        if (pieceType(piece) == KING || m.isPromotion() && pieceType(makePiece(side, PAWN)) == KING) {
            // Wait, this doesn't make sense. Let me fix this.
        }
        if (pieceType(m.isPromotion() ? makePiece(side, PAWN) : piece) == KING) {
            kingSq[side] = from;
        }
        
        // Restore state
        castling = undo.castling;
        epSquare = undo.epSquare;
        halfmove = undo.halfmove;
        hash = undo.hash;
        
        if (side == BLACK) fullmove--;
    }
    
    // ===== Evaluation =====
    int evaluate() const {
        int score = 0;
        
        for (int sq = 0; sq < 64; sq++) {
            int p = board[sq];
            if (p == EMPTY) continue;
            
            int pt = pieceType(p);
            int color = pieceColor(p);
            int sqForPST = (color == WHITE) ? sq : mirrorSquare(sq);
            
            int value = MATERIAL[pt] + PST[pt][sqForPST];
            if (color == WHITE) score += value;
            else score -= value;
        }
        
        return (side == WHITE) ? score : -score;
    }
};

// ===== Transposition Table =====
struct TTEntry {
    uint64_t hash;
    int16_t score;
    uint8_t depth;
    uint8_t flag;
    CompactMove bestMove;
};

const int TT_SIZE = (1 << 24); // 16 million entries
TTEntry* tt = nullptr;

void initTT() {
    tt = new TTEntry[TT_SIZE];
    memset(tt, 0, sizeof(TTEntry) * TT_SIZE);
}

TTEntry* probeTT(uint64_t hash) {
    int idx = hash & (TT_SIZE - 1);
    if (tt[idx].hash == hash) return &tt[idx];
    return nullptr;
}

void storeTT(uint64_t hash, int score, int depth, int flag, CompactMove bestMove) {
    int idx = hash & (TT_SIZE - 1);
    // Replace if deeper or same position
    if (tt[idx].hash == hash || tt[idx].depth <= depth) {
        tt[idx] = { hash, (int16_t)score, (uint8_t)depth, (uint8_t)flag, bestMove };
    }
}

// ===== Search =====
int INF_SCORE = 100000;
int MATE_SCORE = 50000;

// Killer moves
Move killerMoves[64][2];
int historyTable[2][64][64]; // [color][from][to]

void clearSearch() {
    memset(killerMoves, 0, sizeof(killerMoves));
    memset(historyTable, 0, sizeof(historyTable));
}

// Score a move for ordering
int scoreMove(const Position& pos, const Move& m, const Move& ttMove, int ply) {
    // TT move gets highest priority
    if (m.from == ttMove.from && m.to == ttMove.to && m.promotion == ttMove.promotion)
        return 10000000;
    
    // Captures: MVV-LVA
    if (m.isCapture()) {
        int victim = pieceType(m.captured);
        int attacker = pieceType(pos.board[m.from]);
        return 1000000 + MATERIAL[victim] * 10 - MATERIAL[attacker];
    }
    
    // Killer moves
    if (ply < 64) {
        if (m.from == killerMoves[ply][0].from && m.to == killerMoves[ply][0].to && 
            m.promotion == killerMoves[ply][0].promotion)
            return 500000;
        if (m.from == killerMoves[ply][1].from && m.to == killerMoves[ply][1].to && 
            m.promotion == killerMoves[ply][1].promotion)
            return 490000;
    }
    
    // Promotion
    if (m.isPromotion()) return 480000 + MATERIAL[m.promotion];
    
    // History heuristic
    return historyTable[pos.side][m.from][m.to];
}

void orderMoves(const Position& pos, vector<Move>& moves, const Move& ttMove, int ply) {
    vector<int> scores(moves.size());
    for (size_t i = 0; i < moves.size(); i++)
        scores[i] = scoreMove(pos, moves[i], ttMove, ply);
    
    // Simple selection sort (good enough for move ordering since we pick one at a time)
    for (size_t i = 0; i < moves.size(); i++) {
        size_t best = i;
        for (size_t j = i + 1; j < moves.size(); j++) {
            if (scores[j] > scores[best]) best = j;
        }
        if (best != i) {
            swap(moves[i], moves[best]);
            swap(scores[i], scores[best]);
        }
    }
}

// Global timeout flag
atomic<bool> searchTimeout(false);
TimePoint searchStartTime;
int searchTimeLimit; // milliseconds

bool checkTimeout() {
    auto elapsed = chrono::duration_cast<chrono::milliseconds>(Clock::now() - searchStartTime).count();
    return elapsed >= searchTimeLimit;
}

class Searcher {
public:
    Position pos;
    int nodes;
    int maxPly;
    Move bestRootMove;
    
    Searcher() : nodes(0), maxPly(0) {}
    
    int quiescence(int alpha, int beta, int ply) {
        nodes++;
        
        if (nodes % 4096 == 0 && checkTimeout())
            searchTimeout = true;
        if (searchTimeout) return 0;
        
        int standPat = pos.evaluate();
        if (standPat >= beta) return beta;
        if (standPat > alpha) alpha = standPat;
        
        // Delta pruning
        const int DELTA = 900; // queen value
        if (standPat + DELTA < alpha) return alpha;
        
        vector<Move> captures = pos.generateCaptureMoves();
        // For captures, also need to filter for legality
        // But let's just order by MVV-LVA and search
        
        // Order captures by MVV-LVA
        for (auto& m : captures) {
            // Score temporarily stored in flags... no, let me use a different approach
        }
        
        // Simple sort by captured piece value (descending)
        sort(captures.begin(), captures.end(), [](const Move& a, const Move& b) {
            return MATERIAL[pieceType(a.captured)] > MATERIAL[pieceType(b.captured)];
        });
        
        for (const Move& m : captures) {
            pos.makeMove(m);
            if (pos.isSquareAttacked(pos.kingSq[pos.side ^ 1], pos.side)) {
                pos.unmakeMove(m);
                continue; // illegal move
            }
            
            int score = -quiescence(-beta, -alpha, ply + 1);
            pos.unmakeMove(m);
            
            if (searchTimeout) return 0;
            
            if (score >= beta) return beta;
            if (score > alpha) alpha = score;
        }
        
        return alpha;
    }
    
    int alphaBeta(int alpha, int beta, int depth, int ply, bool doNull) {
        if (searchTimeout) return 0;
        
        nodes++;
        if (nodes % 4096 == 0 && checkTimeout()) {
            searchTimeout = true;
            return 0;
        }
        
        bool isRoot = (ply == 0);
        bool inCheck = pos.inCheck();
        
        // Check extension
        if (inCheck) depth++;
        
        if (depth <= 0) {
            return quiescence(alpha, beta, ply);
        }
        
        // Draw by 50-move rule
        if (pos.halfmove >= 100 && !isRoot) return 0;
        
        // Transposition table probe
        CompactMove cmBest = 0;
        TTEntry* tte = probeTT(pos.hash);
        Move ttMove = {0, 0, 0, 0, 0};
        if (tte && tte->hash == pos.hash) {
            cmBest = tte->bestMove;
            ttMove = unpackMove(cmBest);
            if (tte->depth >= depth && !isRoot) {
                int ttScore = tte->score;
                // Adjust mate scores
                if (ttScore > MATE_SCORE - 100) ttScore -= ply;
                if (ttScore < -MATE_SCORE + 100) ttScore += ply;
                
                if (tte->flag == TT_EXACT) return ttScore;
                if (tte->flag == TT_LOWER && ttScore >= beta) return ttScore;
                if (tte->flag == TT_UPPER && ttScore <= alpha) return ttScore;
            }
        }
        
        // Null move pruning
        if (doNull && !inCheck && depth >= 3 && pos.halfmove > 0) {
            // Make null move
            int savedEp = pos.epSquare;
            uint64_t savedHash = pos.hash;
            pos.hash ^= (pos.epSquare >= 0) ? zobEp[fileOf(pos.epSquare)] : 0;
            pos.epSquare = -1;
            pos.hash ^= zobSide;
            pos.side ^= 1;
            
            int R = depth >= 6 ? 3 : 2;
            int score = -alphaBeta(-beta, -beta + 1, depth - 1 - R, ply + 1, false);
            
            // Unmake null move
            pos.side ^= 1;
            pos.epSquare = savedEp;
            pos.hash = savedHash;
            
            if (searchTimeout) return 0;
            
            if (score >= beta) return beta;
        }
        
        // Generate and order moves
        vector<Move> moves = pos.generatePseudoLegalMoves();
        Move orderedTTMove = ttMove;
        orderMoves(pos, moves, orderedTTMove, ply);
        
        int bestScore = -INF_SCORE;
        Move bestMove = {0, 0, 0, 0, 0};
        int flag = TT_UPPER;
        int legalMoves = 0;
        
        for (size_t i = 0; i < moves.size(); i++) {
            const Move& m = moves[i];
            
            pos.makeMove(m);
            if (pos.isSquareAttacked(pos.kingSq[pos.side ^ 1], pos.side)) {
                pos.unmakeMove(m);
                continue;
            }
            
            legalMoves++;
            
            int score;
            // Late move reduction
            if (legalMoves > 4 && depth >= 3 && !m.isCapture() && !m.isPromotion() && !inCheck) {
                int R = (legalMoves > 10) ? 3 : 2;
                score = -alphaBeta(-alpha - 1, -alpha, depth - 1 - R, ply + 1, true);
                if (score > alpha && score < beta)
                    score = -alphaBeta(-beta, -alpha, depth - 1, ply + 1, true);
            } else {
                score = -alphaBeta(-beta, -alpha, depth - 1, ply + 1, true);
            }
            
            pos.unmakeMove(m);
            
            if (searchTimeout) return 0;
            
            if (score > bestScore) {
                bestScore = score;
                bestMove = m;
                
                if (isRoot) {
                    bestRootMove = m;
                }
                
                if (score > alpha) {
                    alpha = score;
                    flag = TT_EXACT;
                    
                    if (score >= beta) {
                        flag = TT_LOWER;
                        
                        // Update killer moves
                        if (!m.isCapture() && ply < 64) {
                            killerMoves[ply][1] = killerMoves[ply][0];
                            killerMoves[ply][0] = m;
                        }
                        
                        // Update history
                        if (!m.isCapture()) {
                            historyTable[pos.side][m.from][m.to] += depth * depth;
                        }
                        
                        break; // Beta cutoff
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        // No legal moves = checkmate or stalemate
        if (legalMoves == 0) {
            if (inCheck) return -MATE_SCORE + ply;
            else return 0; // stalemate
        }
        
        // Store in TT
        storeTT(pos.hash, bestScore, depth, flag, packMove(bestMove));
        
        return bestScore;
    }
    
    Move iterativeDeepening(int timeLimitMs) {
        searchStartTime = Clock::now();
        searchTimeLimit = timeLimitMs;
        searchTimeout = false;
        clearSearch();
        
        bestRootMove = {0, 0, 0, 0, 0};
        
        // Get initial legal moves
        vector<Move> legalMoves = pos.generateLegalMoves();
        if (legalMoves.empty()) {
            return {0, 0, 0, 0, 0}; // No legal moves (shouldn't happen)
        }
        if (legalMoves.size() == 1) {
            return legalMoves[0]; // Only one legal move
        }
        
        bestRootMove = legalMoves[0];
        
        for (int depth = 1; depth <= 100; depth++) {
            nodes = 0;
            
            int score = alphaBeta(-INF_SCORE, INF_SCORE, depth, 0, true);
            
            if (searchTimeout) break;
            
            // Print thinking info to stderr (optional)
            // cerr << "depth " << depth << " score " << score << " nodes " << nodes << endl;
            
            // If we found a forced mate, we can stop
            if (abs(score) > MATE_SCORE - 100) break;
            
            // Check if we have enough time for the next iteration
            auto elapsed = chrono::duration_cast<chrono::milliseconds>(Clock::now() - searchStartTime).count();
            if (elapsed > timeLimitMs / 3) break;
        }
        
        return bestRootMove;
    }
};
```

Let me rewrite the unmake more carefully:

```cpp
void unmakeMove(const Move& m) {
    side ^= 1;
    const UndoInfo& undo = undoStack[--undoCount];
    
    int from = m.from, to = m.to;
    
    // Determine the original piece that was on from-square
    int origPieceType = m.isPromotion() ? PAWN : pieceType(board[to]);
    int origPiece = makePiece(side, origPieceType);
    
    // Move piece back
    board[from] = origPiece;
    
    // Clear or restore destination
    if (m.isEnPassant()) {
        board[to] = EMPTY; // The ep target square was empty
        int capSq = makeSquare(rankOf(from), fileOf(to));
        board[capSq] = m.captured; // Restore the captured pawn
    } else if (m.captured != EMPTY) {
        board[to] = m.captured;
    } else {
        board[to] = EMPTY;
    }
    
    // Handle castling rook
    if (m.isCastling()) {
        int rookFrom, rookTo;
        if (to > from) { // Kingside
            rookFrom = from + 3;
            rookTo = from + 1;
        } else { // Queenside
            rookFrom = from - 4;
            rookTo = from - 1;
        }
        board[rookFrom] = board[rookTo];
        board[rookTo] = EMPTY;
    }
    
    // Restore king position
    if (origPieceType == KING)
        kingSq[side] = from;
    
    // Restore state
    castling = undo.castling;
    epSquare = undo.epSquare;
    halfmove = undo.halfmove;
    hash = undo.hash;
    
    if (side == BLACK) fullmove--;
}
```

- In unmakeMove: place pawn on e5, place captured pawn on d5 (makeSquare(rankOf(36), fileOf(43)) = makeSquare(4, 3) = 35), clear d6

Actually, there's a concern: if the search times out in the middle, the make/unmake calls might not be balanced. Let me make sure that the search always leaves the position in a consistent state.

In my current code, when `searchTimeout` is set, the `alphaBeta` function returns 0. But the makeMove has already been called for the current move. So the unmakeMove won't be called. This means the position will be in an inconsistent state after a timeout.

To fix this, I should make the search robust against timeouts. One approach is to check for timeout before making a move, and if timeout, don't make the move and return.

But even with that, there could be nested calls. Let me think about this differently.

Actually, the issue is that when searchTimeout becomes true, the recursive calls will start returning without unmaking moves. This will corrupt the position.

A common solution is to check the timeout flag frequently, and when it's set, immediately return without making any more moves. The key is to check the flag BEFORE making a move, not after.

Let me restructure the alpha-beta to check the timeout before making each move:

```cpp
int alphaBeta(...) {
    // ... initial checks ...
    
    for (each move m) {
        if (searchTimeout) break; // Don't make any more moves
        
        pos.makeMove(m);
        if (illegal) {
            pos.unmakeMove(m);
            continue;
        }
        
        int score = -alphaBeta(...);
        pos.unmakeMove(m);
        
        if (searchTimeout) break; // Stop evaluating
    }
    
    return bestScore;
}
```

Wait, this still has a problem. If searchTimeout becomes true during the recursive call, the recursive call might not have properly unmade all moves. Let me think again.

Actually, the recursive call itself will check searchTimeout at the start and return 0. So the moves made within the recursive call should have been unmade (because alphaBeta always unmakes the moves it makes). The issue is only at the current level: if searchTimeout is set during a recursive call, the current level's move has already been unmade (because we unmake it right after the recursive call returns), so we're fine.

Wait, let me trace through:

1. alphaBeta is called at ply 0
2. It makes move m1 (ply 0)
3. It calls alphaBeta at ply 1
4. Ply 1 makes move m2 (ply 1)
5. It calls alphaBeta at ply 2
6. Ply 2 checks timeout, finds it's timed out, returns 0
7. Ply 1 unmakes m2, checks timeout, finds it's timed out, breaks out of the loop
8. Ply 0 unmakes m1, checks timeout, finds it's timed out, breaks out of the loop

Wait, but in step 7, after unmaking m2, ply 1 continues with the loop and checks timeout. If timeout is set, it breaks. So the moves at ply 1 that were already made and unmade are fine.

Actually, the issue is more subtle. Let me look at my code again:

```cpp

    pos.makeMove(m);
```

If alphaBeta returns 0 because of timeout, we unmake the move (good) and then break out of the loop. The position should be consistent at this point.

But what if the timeout happens inside alphaBeta at a deeper level? The deeper alphaBeta will unmake all its moves before returning. So when it returns to the current level, the current level's move is still made. We then unmake it and break. So the position should be consistent.

Wait, actually, let me look more carefully. The quiescence search also makes and unmakes moves:

```cpp
// Null move pruning
if (doNull && !inCheck && depth >= 3) {
    uint64_t savedHash = pos.hash;
    int savedEp = pos.epSquare;
    int savedSide = pos.side;
    
    // Update hash for null move
    pos.hash ^= (pos.epSquare >= 0) ? zobEp[fileOf(pos.epSquare)] : 0; // remove EP
    pos.epSquare = -1;
    pos.hash ^= zobSide; // flip side
    pos.side ^= 1;
    
    int R = depth >= 6 ? 3 : 2;
    int score = -alphaBeta(-beta, -beta + 1, depth - 1 - R, ply + 1, false);
    
    // Restore
    pos.side = savedSide;
    pos.epSquare = savedEp;
    pos.hash = savedHash;
    
    if (searchTimeout) return 0;
    if (score >= beta) return beta;
}
```

Actually, I just realized something. The FEN specification says the en passant square is set if and only if a pawn has just made a double push on the previous move. Some strict FEN implementations only set the ep square if an en passant capture is actually possible (i.e., there's an enemy pawn adjacent to the double-pushed pawn). But the standard FEN specification doesn't require this.

For my implementation, I'll just trust the FEN as given. If the ep square is set, I'll store it and generate en passant captures if possible.

One more optimization I want to add: the principal variation search (PVS). Instead of using a full window for all moves, I first search the first move (presumably the best) with a full window, and then search the remaining moves with a null window (-alpha-1, -alpha). If a move fails high (score > alpha), I re-search it with the full window. This can significantly reduce the search time.

But this is already similar to what I'm doing with LMR. Let me combine LMR and PVS.

OK, here's my plan for the alpha-beta search:

```
1. Check for timeout
2. Check extension (if in check)
3. Probe TT
4. Null move pruning
5. Generate and order moves
6. For each move:
   a. Make the move
   b. Check legality
   c. If first move or PV node, search with full window
   d. Otherwise, search with null window (PVS)
   e. If the null window search fails high, re-search with full window
   f. Update alpha, beta, best move
7. Handle checkmate/stalemate
8. Store in TT
```

```cpp

void pushHash() {
    hashHistory[hashHistorySize++] = hash;
}

void popHash() {
    hashHistorySize--;
}

bool isRepetition() const {
    // Check the last halfmove positions
    int start = hashHistorySize - 1 - halfmove;
    if (start < 0) start = 0;
    for (int i = hashHistorySize - 2; i >= start; i--) {

}
```

One important thing about the search: when I detect a timeout, I should return the best move found so far, not the move from the current (incomplete) iteration. My iterative deepening loop handles this correctly: I save `bestRootMove` at each completed iteration, and if the next iteration times out, I use the saved move.

But there's a subtle issue: within an iteration, if the search times out while evaluating the first move at the root, `bestRootMove` might be updated to a move that hasn't been fully evaluated. This could lead to a suboptimal move.

To handle this, I can keep track of the best move from the previous iteration and only update `bestRootMove` after the current iteration completes. But this is overly conservative. A better approach is to update `bestRootMove` after each fully evaluated move at the root, not after the entire iteration.

Actually, in my current code, `bestRootMove` is updated inside `alphaBeta` when `isRoot` is true. This means it's updated after each fully evaluated move at the root. So if the search times out during the third move, `bestRootMove` will be the best move found among the first two moves (or the first move if the second was worse). This is a reasonable approach.

But there's still a risk: if the first move evaluated is bad, and the search times out before evaluating the second move, we'll be stuck with the bad first move. To mitigate this, I should order the moves at the root so that the best move (from the TT or the previous iteration) is evaluated first. This is already handled by my move ordering (TT move gets highest priority).

OK, I think my approach is sound. Let me write the code now.

Actually, one more optimization: I should use aspiration windows in iterative deepening. Instead of searching with a full window (-INF, INF) at each depth, I search with a narrow window around the previous score. If the search fails low or high, I widen the window and re-search.

This can significantly reduce the search time, especially at higher depths. But it adds complexity. Let me add it for robustness.

```cpp
for (int depth = 1; depth <= 100; depth++) {
    int alpha = prevScore - 50;
    int beta = prevScore + 50;
    int score = alphaBeta(alpha, beta, depth, 0, true);
    
    if (score <= alpha || score >= beta) {
        // Re-search with full window
        score = alphaBeta(-INF_SCORE, INF_SCORE, depth, 0, true);
    }
    
    if (searchTimeout) break;
    prevScore = score;
    // ...
}
```

Actually, this is not quite right. If the search fails low or high, I should widen the window gradually, not jump to the full window. But for simplicity, let me just use the full window as a fallback.

Hmm, actually, aspiration windows can be tricky to get right. Let me skip them for now and just use a full window.

Actually, I realize there might be a subtle bug in my sliding piece move generation. When a bishop/rook/queen slides off the edge of the board, the file difference check might not catch all cases. Let me verify:

For a bishop moving diagonally up-left from a1 (sq=0, rank=0, file=0):
offset = -9 (up-left from a1 is invalid, should be off-board)
target = 0 + (-9) = -9 -> onBoard returns false. ✓

For a bishop moving diagonally up-left from b1 (sq=1, rank=0, file=1):
offset = -9 -> target = 1 - 9 = -8 -> onBoard returns false. ✓

For a bishop moving diagonally up-left from a2 (sq=8, rank=1, file=0):
offset = -9 -> target = 8 - 9 = -1 -> onBoard returns false. ✓

For a bishop moving diagonally down-right from h8 (sq=63, rank=7, file=7):
offset = 9 -> target = 63 + 9 = 72 -> onBoard returns false. ✓

For a rook moving right from h1 (sq=7, rank=0, file=7):
offset = 1 -> target = 8 = a2! But we check abs(fileOf(8) - fileOf(7)) = abs(0-7) = 7 > 1, so we break. ✓

For a rook moving left from a1 (sq=0, rank=0, file=0):
offset = -1 -> target = -1 -> onBoard returns false. ✓

Let me also think about one more thing: the format of the output. The problem says:

"Move notation rules:
- Piece letter (lowercase p for pawn, uppercase N/B/R/Q/K for others) + source square + destination square.
- Use "x" between source and destination for captures: pe4xd5
- Promotion: append / and the piece letter, e.g. pe7e8/Q
- Castling: O-O (kingside) or O-O-O (queenside).
- En passant: append ep, e.g. pe5xd6ep
- Check: append +, e.g. Bb4c5+
- Checkmate: append #, e.g. Qd1h5#"

So the format is:
- [piece][source][x?][dest][/promo?][ep?][+|#?]

Let me make sure my formatMove function generates this correctly:

For pe2e4: piece='p', source="e2", no capture, dest="e4"
My code: r = "p" + "e2" + "e4" = "pe2e4" ✓

For pe4xd5: piece='p', source="e4", capture, dest="d5"
My code: r = "p" + "e4" + "x" + "d5" = "pe4xd5" ✓

For pe7e8/Q: piece='p', source="e7", no capture, dest="e8", promo='Q'
My code: r = "p" + "e7" + "e8" + "/" + "Q" = "pe7e8/Q" ✓

For O-O: kingside castling
My code: r = "O-O" ✓

For pe5xd6ep: piece='p', source="e5", capture, dest="d6", ep
My code: r = "p" + "e5" + "x" + "d6" + "ep" = "pe5xd6ep" ✓

For Bb4c5+: piece='B', source="b4", no capture, dest="c5", check
My code: r = "B" + "b4" + "c5" + "+" = "Bb4c5+" ✓

For Qd1h5#: piece='Q', source="d1", no capture, dest="h5", checkmate
My code: r = "Q" + "d1" + "h5" + "#" = "Qd1h5#" ✓

Let me also reconsider the TT implementation. I want to use a replacement strategy that maximizes the usefulness of the TT entries. A simple strategy is to always replace the existing entry with the new one (except if the existing entry has a higher depth). This is called "depth-preferred" replacement.

This only uses the TT entry if the stored depth is >= current depth. Otherwise, it just uses the best move for move ordering. This is correct.

using namespace std;

enum PieceType : int8_t { NO_TYPE = 0, PAWN = 1, KNIGHT = 2, BISHOP = 3, ROOK = 4, QUEEN = 5, KING = 6 };
enum Color : int8_t { WHITE = 0, BLACK = 1 };

inline int8_t makePiece(Color c, PieceType pt) { return (int8_t)(c * 6 + pt); }
inline Color pieceColor(int8_t p) { return (Color)((p - 1) / 6); }
